# Sakuya Cheat Menu Pro - Block 5 Scripted GUIs

sakuya_b5_has_selection_check = {
	scope = country
	is_shown = {
		OR = {
			has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_armed_forces
			has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_devout
			has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_industrialists
			has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_intelligentsia
			has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_landowners
			has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_petty_bourgeoisie
			has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_rural_folk
			has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_trade_unions
		}
	}
}

sakuya_b5_has_single_selection_check = {
	scope = country
	is_shown = {
		OR = {
			AND = { has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_armed_forces NOT = { OR = { has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_devout has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_industrialists has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_intelligentsia has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_landowners has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_petty_bourgeoisie has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_rural_folk has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_trade_unions } } }
			AND = { has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_devout NOT = { OR = { has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_armed_forces has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_industrialists has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_intelligentsia has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_landowners has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_petty_bourgeoisie has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_rural_folk has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_trade_unions } } }
			AND = { has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_industrialists NOT = { OR = { has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_armed_forces has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_devout has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_intelligentsia has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_landowners has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_petty_bourgeoisie has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_rural_folk has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_trade_unions } } }
			AND = { has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_intelligentsia NOT = { OR = { has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_armed_forces has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_devout has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_industrialists has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_landowners has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_petty_bourgeoisie has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_rural_folk has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_trade_unions } } }
			AND = { has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_landowners NOT = { OR = { has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_armed_forces has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_devout has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_industrialists has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_intelligentsia has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_petty_bourgeoisie has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_rural_folk has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_trade_unions } } }
			AND = { has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_petty_bourgeoisie NOT = { OR = { has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_armed_forces has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_devout has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_industrialists has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_intelligentsia has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_landowners has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_rural_folk has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_trade_unions } } }
			AND = { has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_rural_folk NOT = { OR = { has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_armed_forces has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_devout has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_industrialists has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_intelligentsia has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_landowners has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_petty_bourgeoisie has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_trade_unions } } }
			AND = { has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_trade_unions NOT = { OR = { has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_armed_forces has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_devout has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_industrialists has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_intelligentsia has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_landowners has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_petty_bourgeoisie has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_rural_folk } } }
		}
	}
}

sakuya_b5_has_revolution_check = {
	scope = country
	is_shown = {
		OR = {
			has_revolution = yes
			any_political_movement = { is_revolutionary = yes }
			any_political_movement = { is_secessionist = yes }
		}
	}
}

sakuya_b5_has_marked_character_check = {
	scope = country
	is_shown = {
		any_country = {
			any_scope_character = {
				has_variable = sakuya_mark_character_target
			}
		}
	}
}

sakuya_b5_has_selection_and_revolution_check = {
	scope = country
	is_shown = {
		OR = {
			has_revolution = yes
			any_political_movement = { is_revolutionary = yes }
			any_political_movement = { is_secessionist = yes }
		}
		OR = {
			has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_armed_forces
			has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_devout
			has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_industrialists
			has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_intelligentsia
			has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_landowners
			has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_petty_bourgeoisie
			has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_rural_folk
			has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_trade_unions
		}
	}
}

sakuya_b5_has_selection_and_marked_character_check = {
	scope = country
	is_shown = {
		OR = {
			has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_armed_forces
			has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_devout
			has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_industrialists
			has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_intelligentsia
			has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_landowners
			has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_petty_bourgeoisie
			has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_rural_folk
			has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_trade_unions
		}
		any_country = {
			any_scope_character = {
				has_variable = sakuya_mark_character_target
			}
		}
	}
}

sakuya_b5_select_armed_forces_check = { scope = country is_shown = { has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_armed_forces } }
sakuya_b5_select_armed_forces_toggle = { scope = country is_shown = { is_player = yes } effect = { if = { limit = { has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_armed_forces } remove_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_armed_forces } else = { set_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_armed_forces } } }
sakuya_b5_select_armed_forces_solo = { scope = country is_shown = { is_player = yes } effect = { remove_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_armed_forces remove_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_devout remove_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_industrialists remove_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_intelligentsia remove_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_landowners remove_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_petty_bourgeoisie remove_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_rural_folk remove_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_trade_unions set_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_armed_forces } }

sakuya_b5_select_mages_check = {
    scope = country
    is_shown = {
        is_player = yes
        exists = ig:ig_mages
        NOT = { has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_mages }
    }
}

sakuya_b5_select_mages_toggle = {
    scope = country
    is_shown = {
        is_player = yes
        exists = ig:ig_mages
    }
    effect = {
        if = {
            limit = { NOT = { has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_mages } }
            remove_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_armed_forces
            remove_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_devout
            remove_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_industrialists
            remove_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_intelligentsia
            remove_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_landowners
            remove_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_petty_bourgeoisie
            remove_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_rural_folk
            remove_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_trade_unions
            remove_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_clans
            set_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_mages
        }
        else = { remove_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_mages }
    }
}

sakuya_b5_select_mages_solo = {
    scope = country
    is_shown = { is_player = yes exists = ig:ig_mages }
    effect = {
        remove_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_armed_forces
        remove_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_devout
        remove_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_industrialists
        remove_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_intelligentsia
        remove_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_landowners
        remove_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_petty_bourgeoisie
        remove_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_rural_folk
        remove_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_trade_unions
        remove_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_clans
        set_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_mages
    }
}

sakuya_b5_select_clans_check = {
    scope = country
    is_shown = {
        is_player = yes
        exists = ig:ig_clans
        NOT = { has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_clans }
    }
}

sakuya_b5_select_clans_toggle = {
    scope = country
    is_shown = {
        is_player = yes
        exists = ig:ig_clans
    }
    effect = {
        if = {
            limit = { NOT = { has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_clans } }
            remove_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_armed_forces
            remove_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_devout
            remove_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_industrialists
            remove_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_intelligentsia
            remove_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_landowners
            remove_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_petty_bourgeoisie
            remove_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_rural_folk
            remove_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_trade_unions
            remove_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_mages
            set_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_clans
        }
        else = { remove_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_clans }
    }
}

sakuya_b5_select_clans_solo = {
    scope = country
    is_shown = { is_player = yes exists = ig:ig_clans }
    effect = {
        remove_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_armed_forces
        remove_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_devout
        remove_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_industrialists
        remove_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_intelligentsia
        remove_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_landowners
        remove_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_petty_bourgeoisie
        remove_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_rural_folk
        remove_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_trade_unions
        remove_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_mages
        set_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_clans
    }
}

sakuya_b5_all_approval_check = { scope = country is_shown = { has_variable = sakuya_b5_all_approval_active } }
sakuya_b5_all_approval_add = {
	scope = country
	is_shown = { is_player = yes }
	effect = {
		if = { limit = { NOT = { has_variable = sakuya_b5_all_approval_mult } } set_variable = { name = sakuya_b5_all_approval_mult value = 0 } }
		change_variable = { name = sakuya_b5_all_approval_mult add = 5 }
		remove_modifier = sakuya_cheat_b5_all_approval
		if = { limit = { has_variable = sakuya_b5_all_approval_mult } add_modifier = { name = sakuya_cheat_b5_all_approval multiplier = var:sakuya_b5_all_approval_mult } set_variable = sakuya_b5_all_approval_active }
		if = { limit = { var:sakuya_b5_all_approval_mult = 0 } remove_modifier = sakuya_cheat_b5_all_approval remove_variable = sakuya_b5_all_approval_mult remove_variable = sakuya_b5_all_approval_active }
	}
}
sakuya_b5_all_approval_add_shift = {
	scope = country
	is_shown = { is_player = yes }
	effect = {
		if = { limit = { NOT = { has_variable = sakuya_b5_all_approval_mult } } set_variable = { name = sakuya_b5_all_approval_mult value = 0 } }
		change_variable = { name = sakuya_b5_all_approval_mult add = 100 }
		remove_modifier = sakuya_cheat_b5_all_approval
		add_modifier = { name = sakuya_cheat_b5_all_approval multiplier = var:sakuya_b5_all_approval_mult }
		set_variable = sakuya_b5_all_approval_active
	}
}
sakuya_b5_all_approval_add_alt = {
	scope = country
	is_shown = { is_player = yes }
	effect = {
		if = { limit = { NOT = { has_variable = sakuya_b5_all_approval_mult } } set_variable = { name = sakuya_b5_all_approval_mult value = 0 } }
		change_variable = { name = sakuya_b5_all_approval_mult add = 1 }
		remove_modifier = sakuya_cheat_b5_all_approval
		add_modifier = { name = sakuya_cheat_b5_all_approval multiplier = var:sakuya_b5_all_approval_mult }
		set_variable = sakuya_b5_all_approval_active
	}
}
sakuya_b5_all_approval_sub = {
	scope = country
	is_shown = { is_player = yes }
	effect = {
		if = { limit = { NOT = { has_variable = sakuya_b5_all_approval_mult } } set_variable = { name = sakuya_b5_all_approval_mult value = 0 } }
		change_variable = { name = sakuya_b5_all_approval_mult add = -5 }
		remove_modifier = sakuya_cheat_b5_all_approval
		if = { limit = { has_variable = sakuya_b5_all_approval_mult } add_modifier = { name = sakuya_cheat_b5_all_approval multiplier = var:sakuya_b5_all_approval_mult } set_variable = sakuya_b5_all_approval_active }
		if = { limit = { var:sakuya_b5_all_approval_mult = 0 } remove_modifier = sakuya_cheat_b5_all_approval remove_variable = sakuya_b5_all_approval_mult remove_variable = sakuya_b5_all_approval_active }
	}
}
sakuya_b5_all_approval_clear = { scope = country is_shown = { is_player = yes } effect = { remove_modifier = sakuya_cheat_b5_all_approval remove_variable = sakuya_b5_all_approval_mult remove_variable = sakuya_b5_all_approval_active } }

sakuya_b5_all_pol_str_mult_check = { scope = country is_shown = { has_variable = sakuya_b5_all_pol_str_mult_active } }
sakuya_b5_all_pol_str_mult_add = {
	scope = country
	is_shown = { is_player = yes }
	effect = {
		if = { limit = { NOT = { has_variable = sakuya_b5_all_pol_str_mult_value } } set_variable = { name = sakuya_b5_all_pol_str_mult_value value = 0 } }
		change_variable = { name = sakuya_b5_all_pol_str_mult_value add = 0.2 }
		remove_modifier = sakuya_cheat_b5_all_pol_str_mult

	scope = country

	effect = {
		if = { limit = { NOT = { has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_approval_mult } } set_variable = { name = sakuya_b5_sel_approval_mult value = 0 } }

		if = { limit = { has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_devout } remove_modifier = sakuya_cheat_b5_devout_approval if = { limit = { has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_approval_mult } add_modifier = { name = sakuya_cheat_b5_devout_approval multiplier = var:sakuya_b5_sel_approval_mult } } }
		if = { limit = { has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_industrialists } remove_modifier = sakuya_cheat_b5_industrialists_approval if = { limit = { has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_approval_mult } add_modifier = { name = sakuya_cheat_b5_industrialists_approval multiplier = var:sakuya_b5_sel_approval_mult } } }
		if = { limit = { has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_intelligentsia } remove_modifier = sakuya_cheat_b5_intelligentsia_approval if = { limit = { has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_approval_mult } add_modifier = { name = sakuya_cheat_b5_intelligentsia_approval multiplier = var:sakuya_b5_sel_approval_mult } } }
		if = { limit = { has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_landowners } remove_modifier = sakuya_cheat_b5_landowners_approval if = { limit = { has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_approval_mult } add_modifier = { name = sakuya_cheat_b5_landowners_approval multiplier = var:sakuya_b5_sel_approval_mult } } }
		if = { limit = { has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_petty_bourgeoisie } remove_modifier = sakuya_cheat_b5_petty_bourgeoisie_approval if = { limit = { has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_approval_mult } add_modifier = { name = sakuya_cheat_b5_petty_bourgeoisie_approval multiplier = var:sakuya_b5_sel_approval_mult } } }

		if = { limit = { var:sakuya_b5_sel_approval_mult = 0 } remove_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_approval_mult remove_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_approval_active }
		else = { set_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_approval_active }

		remove_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_amenability_active
	}
}

		if = { limit = { has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_rural_folk } add_loyalists = { value = 1.0 interest_group = ig:ig_rural_folk } }

	}
}

		if = { limit = { has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_trade_unions } ig:ig_trade_unions = { remove_ideology = ideology_republican } }
	}
}

sakuya_b5_fx_set_marked_character_as_ig_leader = {
	scope = country
	is_shown = { is_player = yes }
	effect = {
		remove_variable = sakuya_b5_marked_character_ready
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				any_scope_character = {
					has_variable = sakuya_mark_character_target
				}
			}
			every_scope_character = {
				limit = { has_variable = sakuya_mark_character_target }
				save_scope_as = sakuya_b5_marked_character_scope
				set_variable = sakuya_b5_marked_character_ready
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = sakuya_b5_marked_character_ready
				exists = scope:sakuya_b5_marked_character_scope
				has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_armed_forces
				scope:sakuya_b5_marked_character_scope.interest_group = { is_same_interest_group_type = ig:ig_armed_forces }
			}
			scope:sakuya_b5_marked_character_scope = { set_as_interest_group_leader = yes }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = sakuya_b5_marked_character_ready
				exists = scope:sakuya_b5_marked_character_scope
				has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_devout
				scope:sakuya_b5_marked_character_scope.interest_group = { is_same_interest_group_type = ig:ig_devout }
			}
			scope:sakuya_b5_marked_character_scope = { set_as_interest_group_leader = yes }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = sakuya_b5_marked_character_ready
				exists = scope:sakuya_b5_marked_character_scope
				has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_industrialists
				scope:sakuya_b5_marked_character_scope.interest_group = { is_same_interest_group_type = ig:ig_industrialists }
			}
			scope:sakuya_b5_marked_character_scope = { set_as_interest_group_leader = yes }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = sakuya_b5_marked_character_ready
				exists = scope:sakuya_b5_marked_character_scope
				has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_intelligentsia
				scope:sakuya_b5_marked_character_scope.interest_group = { is_same_interest_group_type = ig:ig_intelligentsia }
			}
			scope:sakuya_b5_marked_character_scope = { set_as_interest_group_leader = yes }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = sakuya_b5_marked_character_ready
				exists = scope:sakuya_b5_marked_character_scope
				has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_landowners
				scope:sakuya_b5_marked_character_scope.interest_group = { is_same_interest_group_type = ig:ig_landowners }
			}
			scope:sakuya_b5_marked_character_scope = { set_as_interest_group_leader = yes }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = sakuya_b5_marked_character_ready
				exists = scope:sakuya_b5_marked_character_scope
				has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_petty_bourgeoisie
				scope:sakuya_b5_marked_character_scope.interest_group = { is_same_interest_group_type = ig:ig_petty_bourgeoisie }
			}
			scope:sakuya_b5_marked_character_scope = { set_as_interest_group_leader = yes }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = sakuya_b5_marked_character_ready
				exists = scope:sakuya_b5_marked_character_scope
				has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_rural_folk
				scope:sakuya_b5_marked_character_scope.interest_group = { is_same_interest_group_type = ig:ig_rural_folk }
			}
			scope:sakuya_b5_marked_character_scope = { set_as_interest_group_leader = yes }
		}
		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = sakuya_b5_marked_character_ready
				exists = scope:sakuya_b5_marked_character_scope
				has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_trade_unions
				scope:sakuya_b5_marked_character_scope.interest_group = { is_same_interest_group_type = ig:ig_trade_unions }
			}
			scope:sakuya_b5_marked_character_scope = { set_as_interest_group_leader = yes }
		}
		remove_variable = sakuya_b5_marked_character_ready
	}
}

sakuya_b5_fx_set_leader_ideology_moderate = {
	scope = country
	is_shown = { is_player = yes }
	effect = {
		if = { limit = { has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_armed_forces } ig:ig_armed_forces = { leader = { set_ideology = ideology:ideology_moderate } } }
		if = { limit = { has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_devout } ig:ig_devout = { leader = { set_ideology = ideology:ideology_moderate } } }
		if = { limit = { has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_industrialists } ig:ig_industrialists = { leader = { set_ideology = ideology:ideology_moderate } } }
		if = { limit = { has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_intelligentsia } ig:ig_intelligentsia = { leader = { set_ideology = ideology:ideology_moderate } } }
		if = { limit = { has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_landowners } ig:ig_landowners = { leader = { set_ideology = ideology:ideology_moderate } } }
		if = { limit = { has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_petty_bourgeoisie } ig:ig_petty_bourgeoisie = { leader = { set_ideology = ideology:ideology_moderate } } }
		if = { limit = { has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_rural_folk } ig:ig_rural_folk = { leader = { set_ideology = ideology:ideology_moderate } } }
		if = { limit = { has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_trade_unions } ig:ig_trade_unions = { leader = { set_ideology = ideology:ideology_moderate } } }
	}
}

sakuya_b5_fx_create_leader_moderate = {
	scope = country
	is_shown = { is_player = yes }
	effect = {
		if = { limit = { has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_armed_forces } create_character = { interest_group = ig:ig_armed_forces culture = primary_culture ideology = ideology_moderate on_created = { set_as_interest_group_leader = yes } } }
		if = { limit = { has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_devout } create_character = { interest_group = ig:ig_devout culture = primary_culture ideology = ideology_moderate on_created = { set_as_interest_group_leader = yes } } }
		if = { limit = { has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_industrialists } create_character = { interest_group = ig:ig_industrialists culture = primary_culture ideology = ideology_moderate on_created = { set_as_interest_group_leader = yes } } }
		if = { limit = { has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_intelligentsia } create_character = { interest_group = ig:ig_intelligentsia culture = primary_culture ideology = ideology_moderate on_created = { set_as_interest_group_leader = yes } } }
		if = { limit = { has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_landowners } create_character = { interest_group = ig:ig_landowners culture = primary_culture ideology = ideology_moderate on_created = { set_as_interest_group_leader = yes } } }
		if = { limit = { has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_petty_bourgeoisie } create_character = { interest_group = ig:ig_petty_bourgeoisie culture = primary_culture ideology = ideology_moderate on_created = { set_as_interest_group_leader = yes } } }

		if = { limit = { has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_petty_bourgeoisie } ig:ig_petty_bourgeoisie = { leader = { remove_as_interest_group_leader = yes } } }
		if = { limit = { has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_rural_folk } ig:ig_rural_folk = { leader = { remove_as_interest_group_leader = yes } } }
		if = { limit = { has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_trade_unions } ig:ig_trade_unions = { leader = { remove_as_interest_group_leader = yes } } }
	}
}

sakuya_b5_fx_set_ig_trait_engines_of_progress = {
	scope = country
	is_shown = { is_player = yes }
	effect = {
		if = { limit = { has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_armed_forces } ig:ig_armed_forces = { set_ig_trait = ig_trait:ig_trait_engines_of_progress } }

    is_shown = { is_player = yes }
    effect = {
        if = { limit = { has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_armed_forces } ig:ig_armed_forces = { set_ig_trait = ig_trait:ig_trait_avant_garde } }
        if = { limit = { has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_devout } ig:ig_devout = { set_ig_trait = ig_trait:ig_trait_avant_garde } }
        if = { limit = { has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_industrialists } ig:ig_industrialists = { set_ig_trait = ig_trait:ig_trait_avant_garde } }
        if = { limit = { has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_intelligentsia } ig:ig_intelligentsia = { set_ig_trait = ig_trait:ig_trait_avant_garde } }
        if = { limit = { has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_landowners } ig:ig_landowners = { set_ig_trait = ig_trait:ig_trait_avant_garde } }
        if = { limit = { has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_petty_bourgeoisie } ig:ig_petty_bourgeoisie = { set_ig_trait = ig_trait:ig_trait_avant_garde } }
        if = { limit = { has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_rural_folk } ig:ig_rural_folk = { set_ig_trait = ig_trait:ig_trait_avant_garde } }
        if = { limit = { has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_trade_unions } ig:ig_trade_unions = { set_ig_trait = ig_trait:ig_trait_avant_garde } }
    }
}

    scope = country
    is_shown = { is_player = yes }

        if = { limit = { has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_intelligentsia } ig:ig_intelligentsia = { set_ig_trait = ig_trait:ig_trait_bachareis } }
        if = { limit = { has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_landowners } ig:ig_landowners = { set_ig_trait = ig_trait:ig_trait_bachareis } }
        if = { limit = { has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_petty_bourgeoisie } ig:ig_petty_bourgeoisie = { set_ig_trait = ig_trait:ig_trait_bachareis } }
        if = { limit = { has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_rural_folk } ig:ig_rural_folk = { set_ig_trait = ig_trait:ig_trait_bachareis } }
        if = { limit = { has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_trade_unions } ig:ig_trade_unions = { set_ig_trait = ig_trait:ig_trait_bachareis } }
    }
}

        if = { limit = { has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_petty_bourgeoisie } ig:ig_petty_bourgeoisie = { set_ig_trait = ig_trait:ig_trait_of_the_sovereign_alone } }
        if = { limit = { has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_rural_folk } ig:ig_rural_folk = { set_ig_trait = ig_trait:ig_trait_of_the_sovereign_alone } }
        if = { limit = { has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_trade_unions } ig:ig_trade_unions = { set_ig_trait = ig_trait:ig_trait_of_the_sovereign_alone } }
    }
}

# === Tab 3: 游说团选择 ===

# 检查是否已选中游说团
sakuya_b5_lobby_selected_check = {
	scope = country
	is_shown = {
		any_political_lobby = {
			has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_lobby
		}
	}
}

# 左键：打开选择本国游说团事件
sakuya_b5_lobby_select_open = {
	scope = country
	is_shown = { is_player = yes }
	effect = {
		remove_variable = sakuya_main_force_show
		remove_variable = sakuya_b5_lobby_use_marked_country
		remove_variable = sakuya_b5_lobby_force_empty_notice
		trigger_event = { id = sakuya_main_03_01.2 popup = yes }
	}
}

# 右键：打开选择标记国游说团事件
sakuya_b5_lobby_select_open_marked = {
	scope = country
	is_shown = { is_player = yes }
	effect = {
		save_scope_as = sakuya_b5_root_country_scope
		remove_variable = sakuya_main_force_show
		remove_variable = sakuya_b5_lobby_mark_country_found
		remove_variable = sakuya_b5_lobby_use_marked_country
		remove_variable = sakuya_b5_lobby_force_empty_notice

		every_country = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = sakuya_mark_country_target
			}
			scope:sakuya_b5_root_country_scope = { set_variable = sakuya_b5_lobby_mark_country_found }
			save_scope_as = sakuya_b5_lobby_marked_country_scope
		}

		if = {
			limit = {
				has_variable = sakuya_b5_lobby_mark_country_found
				exists = scope:sakuya_b5_lobby_marked_country_scope
			}
			set_variable = sakuya_b5_lobby_use_marked_country
			trigger_event = { id = sakuya_main_03_01.2 popup = yes }
		}
		else = {
			set_variable = sakuya_b5_lobby_force_empty_notice
			trigger_event = { id = sakuya_main_03_01.2 popup = yes }
		}

		remove_variable = sakuya_b5_lobby_mark_country_found
	}
}

# 取消选择：全局清除所有游说团的选中变量
sakuya_b5_lobby_deselect = {
	scope = country
	is_shown = { is_player = yes }
	effect = {
		every_political_lobby = {
			limit = { has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_lobby }
			remove_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_lobby
		}
		every_country = {
			limit = {
				any_political_lobby = {
					has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_lobby
				}
			}
			every_political_lobby = {
				limit = { has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_lobby }
				remove_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_lobby
			}
		}
	}
}

# === Tab 3 游说团功能 ===

# 检查：全球范围内是否有选中的游说团
sakuya_b5_lobby_selected_global_check = {
	scope = country
	is_shown = {
		OR = {
			any_political_lobby = { has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_lobby }
			any_country = { any_political_lobby = { has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_lobby } }
		}
	}
}

# 检查：游说团 + 利益集团均已选择
sakuya_b5_lobby_and_ig_check = {
	scope = country
	is_shown = {
		OR = {
			any_political_lobby = { has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_lobby }
			any_country = { any_political_lobby = { has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_lobby } }
		}
		OR = {
			has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_armed_forces
			has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_devout
			has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_industrialists
			has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_intelligentsia
			has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_landowners
			has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_petty_bourgeoisie
			has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_rural_folk
			has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_trade_unions
		}
	}
}

# 检查：有标记的目标国家
sakuya_b5_has_marked_country_check = {
	scope = country
	is_shown = {
		any_country = { has_variable = sakuya_mark_country_target }
	}
}

# 检查：杠杆加速修正是否激活
sakuya_b5_lobby_leverage_check = {
	scope = country
	is_shown = {
		has_variable = sakuya_b5_lobby_leverage_active
	}
}

# === 按钮1: 解散选中的游说团 ===
sakuya_b5_lobby_disband = {
	scope = country
	is_shown = { is_player = yes }
	effect = {
		every_country = {
			every_political_lobby = {
				limit = { has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_lobby }
				remove_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_lobby
				disband_political_lobby = yes
			}
		}
	}
}

# === 按钮2: 利益集团加入游说团 ===
sakuya_b5_lobby_ig_join = {
	scope = country
	is_shown = { is_player = yes }
	effect = {
		every_country = {
			if = {
				limit = { any_political_lobby = { has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_lobby } }
				if = { limit = { root = { has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_armed_forces } } ig:ig_armed_forces = { save_scope_as = sakuya_b5_tmp_ig } every_political_lobby = { limit = { has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_lobby } add_lobby_member = scope:sakuya_b5_tmp_ig } }
				if = { limit = { root = { has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_devout } } ig:ig_devout = { save_scope_as = sakuya_b5_tmp_ig } every_political_lobby = { limit = { has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_lobby } add_lobby_member = scope:sakuya_b5_tmp_ig } }
				if = { limit = { root = { has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_industrialists } } ig:ig_industrialists = { save_scope_as = sakuya_b5_tmp_ig } every_political_lobby = { limit = { has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_lobby } add_lobby_member = scope:sakuya_b5_tmp_ig } }
				if = { limit = { root = { has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_intelligentsia } } ig:ig_intelligentsia = { save_scope_as = sakuya_b5_tmp_ig } every_political_lobby = { limit = { has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_lobby } add_lobby_member = scope:sakuya_b5_tmp_ig } }
				if = { limit = { root = { has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_landowners } } ig:ig_landowners = { save_scope_as = sakuya_b5_tmp_ig } every_political_lobby = { limit = { has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_lobby } add_lobby_member = scope:sakuya_b5_tmp_ig } }
				if = { limit = { root = { has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_petty_bourgeoisie } } ig:ig_petty_bourgeoisie = { save_scope_as = sakuya_b5_tmp_ig } every_political_lobby = { limit = { has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_lobby } add_lobby_member = scope:sakuya_b5_tmp_ig } }
				if = { limit = { root = { has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_rural_folk } } ig:ig_rural_folk = { save_scope_as = sakuya_b5_tmp_ig } every_political_lobby = { limit = { has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_lobby } add_lobby_member = scope:sakuya_b5_tmp_ig } }
				if = { limit = { root = { has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_trade_unions } } ig:ig_trade_unions = { save_scope_as = sakuya_b5_tmp_ig } every_political_lobby = { limit = { has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_lobby } add_lobby_member = scope:sakuya_b5_tmp_ig } }
			}
		}
	}
}

# === 按钮2 右键: 利益集团离开游说团 ===
sakuya_b5_lobby_ig_leave = {
	scope = country
	is_shown = { is_player = yes }
	effect = {
		every_country = {
			if = {
				limit = { any_political_lobby = { has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_lobby } }
				if = { limit = { root = { has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_armed_forces } } ig:ig_armed_forces = { save_scope_as = sakuya_b5_tmp_ig } every_political_lobby = { limit = { has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_lobby } remove_lobby_member = scope:sakuya_b5_tmp_ig } }
				if = { limit = { root = { has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_devout } } ig:ig_devout = { save_scope_as = sakuya_b5_tmp_ig } every_political_lobby = { limit = { has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_lobby } remove_lobby_member = scope:sakuya_b5_tmp_ig } }
				if = { limit = { root = { has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_industrialists } } ig:ig_industrialists = { save_scope_as = sakuya_b5_tmp_ig } every_political_lobby = { limit = { has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_lobby } remove_lobby_member = scope:sakuya_b5_tmp_ig } }
				if = { limit = { root = { has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_intelligentsia } } ig:ig_intelligentsia = { save_scope_as = sakuya_b5_tmp_ig } every_political_lobby = { limit = { has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_lobby } remove_lobby_member = scope:sakuya_b5_tmp_ig } }
				if = { limit = { root = { has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_landowners } } ig:ig_landowners = { save_scope_as = sakuya_b5_tmp_ig } every_political_lobby = { limit = { has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_lobby } remove_lobby_member = scope:sakuya_b5_tmp_ig } }
				if = { limit = { root = { has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_petty_bourgeoisie } } ig:ig_petty_bourgeoisie = { save_scope_as = sakuya_b5_tmp_ig } every_political_lobby = { limit = { has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_lobby } remove_lobby_member = scope:sakuya_b5_tmp_ig } }
				if = { limit = { root = { has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_rural_folk } } ig:ig_rural_folk = { save_scope_as = sakuya_b5_tmp_ig } every_political_lobby = { limit = { has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_lobby } remove_lobby_member = scope:sakuya_b5_tmp_ig } }
				if = { limit = { root = { has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_trade_unions } } ig:ig_trade_unions = { save_scope_as = sakuya_b5_tmp_ig } every_political_lobby = { limit = { has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_lobby } remove_lobby_member = scope:sakuya_b5_tmp_ig } }
			}
		}
	}
}

# === 按钮3: 安抚 +3 ===
sakuya_b5_lobby_appease = {
	scope = country
	is_shown = { is_player = yes }
	effect = {
		every_country = { every_political_lobby = { limit = { has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_lobby } change_appeasement = { amount = 3 factor = appeasement_lobby_pleased } } }
	}
}

# === 按钮3 shift: 安抚 +10 ===
sakuya_b5_lobby_appease_shift = {
	scope = country
	is_shown = { is_player = yes }
	effect = {
		every_country = { every_political_lobby = { limit = { has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_lobby } change_appeasement = { amount = 10 factor = appeasement_lobby_pleased } } }
	}
}

# === 按钮3 右键: 激怒 -3 ===
sakuya_b5_lobby_anger = {
	scope = country
	is_shown = { is_player = yes }
	effect = {
		every_country = { every_political_lobby = { limit = { has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_lobby } change_appeasement = { amount = -3 factor = appeasement_lobby_displeased } } }
	}
}

# === 按钮3 alt: 激怒 -10 ===

	scope = country
	is_shown = { is_player = yes }
	effect = {
		every_country = { every_political_lobby = { limit = { has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_lobby } change_appeasement = { amount = -10 factor = appeasement_lobby_displeased } } }

# === 按钮4: 全员加入游说团 ===
sakuya_b5_lobby_add_all = {
	scope = country
	is_shown = { is_player = yes }
	effect = {
		every_country = {
			if = {
				limit = { any_political_lobby = { has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_lobby } }
				every_interest_group = {
					save_scope_as = sakuya_b5_tmp_ig
					prev = {
						every_political_lobby = {
							limit = { has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_lobby }
							add_lobby_member = scope:sakuya_b5_tmp_ig
						}
					}
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

# === 按钮4 右键: 清空游说团全部成员 ===
sakuya_b5_lobby_remove_all = {
	scope = country
	is_shown = { is_player = yes }
	effect = {
		every_country = {
			every_political_lobby = {
				limit = { has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_lobby }
				every_lobby_member = {
					save_scope_as = sakuya_b5_tmp_member
					prev = { remove_lobby_member = scope:sakuya_b5_tmp_member }
				}
			}
		}
	}
}

# === 按钮5: 解散本国所有游说团 ===
sakuya_b5_lobby_disband_all = {
	scope = country
	is_shown = { is_player = yes }
	effect = {
		every_political_lobby = {
			disband_political_lobby = yes
		}
	}
}

# === 按钮5 右键: 解散标记国所有游说团 ===
sakuya_b5_lobby_disband_all_marked = {
	scope = country
	is_shown = { is_player = yes }
	effect = {
		every_country = {
			limit = { has_variable = sakuya_mark_country_target }
			every_political_lobby = {
				disband_political_lobby = yes
			}
		}
	}
}

# === 按钮6: 成立亲目标国游说团（本国） ===
sakuya_b5_lobby_create_pro = {
	scope = country
	is_shown = { is_player = yes }
	effect = {
		every_country = {
			limit = { has_variable = sakuya_mark_country_target }
			save_scope_as = sakuya_b5_target_for_lobby
		}
		if = {
			limit = { exists = scope:sakuya_b5_target_for_lobby }
			if = { limit = { has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_armed_forces } ig:ig_armed_forces = { save_scope_as = sakuya_b5_ig_for_lobby } }
			else_if = { limit = { has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_devout } ig:ig_devout = { save_scope_as = sakuya_b5_ig_for_lobby } }
			else_if = { limit = { has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_industrialists } ig:ig_industrialists = { save_scope_as = sakuya_b5_ig_for_lobby } }
			else_if = { limit = { has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_intelligentsia } ig:ig_intelligentsia = { save_scope_as = sakuya_b5_ig_for_lobby } }
			else_if = { limit = { has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_landowners } ig:ig_landowners = { save_scope_as = sakuya_b5_ig_for_lobby } }
			else_if = { limit = { has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_petty_bourgeoisie } ig:ig_petty_bourgeoisie = { save_scope_as = sakuya_b5_ig_for_lobby } }
			else_if = { limit = { has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_rural_folk } ig:ig_rural_folk = { save_scope_as = sakuya_b5_ig_for_lobby } }
			else_if = { limit = { has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_trade_unions } ig:ig_trade_unions = { save_scope_as = sakuya_b5_ig_for_lobby } }
			else = { random_interest_group = { save_scope_as = sakuya_b5_ig_for_lobby } }
			create_political_lobby = {
				type = lobby_pro_country
				target = scope:sakuya_b5_target_for_lobby
				add_interest_group = scope:sakuya_b5_ig_for_lobby
				lobby_formation_reason = funded
			}
		}
	}
}

# === 按钮6 右键: 成立反目标国游说团（本国） ===
sakuya_b5_lobby_create_anti = {
	scope = country
	is_shown = { is_player = yes }
	effect = {
		every_country = {
			limit = { has_variable = sakuya_mark_country_target }
			save_scope_as = sakuya_b5_target_for_lobby
		}
		if = {
			limit = { exists = scope:sakuya_b5_target_for_lobby }
			if = { limit = { has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_armed_forces } ig:ig_armed_forces = { save_scope_as = sakuya_b5_ig_for_lobby } }
			else_if = { limit = { has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_devout } ig:ig_devout = { save_scope_as = sakuya_b5_ig_for_lobby } }
			else_if = { limit = { has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_industrialists } ig:ig_industrialists = { save_scope_as = sakuya_b5_ig_for_lobby } }
			else_if = { limit = { has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_intelligentsia } ig:ig_intelligentsia = { save_scope_as = sakuya_b5_ig_for_lobby } }
			else_if = { limit = { has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_landowners } ig:ig_landowners = { save_scope_as = sakuya_b5_ig_for_lobby } }
			else_if = { limit = { has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_petty_bourgeoisie } ig:ig_petty_bourgeoisie = { save_scope_as = sakuya_b5_ig_for_lobby } }
			else_if = { limit = { has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_rural_folk } ig:ig_rural_folk = { save_scope_as = sakuya_b5_ig_for_lobby } }
			else_if = { limit = { has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_ig_trade_unions } ig:ig_trade_unions = { save_scope_as = sakuya_b5_ig_for_lobby } }
			else = { random_interest_group = { save_scope_as = sakuya_b5_ig_for_lobby } }
			create_political_lobby = {
				type = lobby_anti_country
				target = scope:sakuya_b5_target_for_lobby
				add_interest_group = scope:sakuya_b5_ig_for_lobby
				lobby_formation_reason = funded
			}
		}
	}
}

# === 按钮6 shift: 在目标国成立亲玩家游说团 ===
sakuya_b5_lobby_create_pro_in_target = {
	scope = country
	is_shown = { is_player = yes }
	effect = {
		save_scope_as = sakuya_b5_player_country
		every_country = {
			limit = { has_variable = sakuya_mark_country_target }
			random_interest_group = { save_scope_as = sakuya_b5_ig_for_lobby }
			create_political_lobby = {
				type = lobby_pro_country
				target = scope:sakuya_b5_player_country
				add_interest_group = scope:sakuya_b5_ig_for_lobby
				lobby_formation_reason = funded
			}
		}
	}
}

# === 按钮6 alt: 在目标国成立反玩家游说团 ===
sakuya_b5_lobby_create_anti_in_target = {
	scope = country
	is_shown = { is_player = yes }
	effect = {
		save_scope_as = sakuya_b5_player_country
		every_country = {
			limit = { has_variable = sakuya_mark_country_target }
			random_interest_group = { save_scope_as = sakuya_b5_ig_for_lobby }
			create_political_lobby = {
				type = lobby_anti_country
				target = scope:sakuya_b5_player_country
				add_interest_group = scope:sakuya_b5_ig_for_lobby
				lobby_formation_reason = funded
			}
		}
	}
}

# === 按钮7: 转换游说团类型（亲↔反） ===
sakuya_b5_lobby_swap_type = {
	scope = country
	is_shown = { is_player = yes }
	effect = {
		every_country = {
			every_political_lobby = {
				limit = { has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_lobby }
				target = { save_scope_as = sakuya_b5_swap_target }
				save_scope_as = sakuya_b5_swap_lobby
				if = { limit = { is_political_lobby_type = lobby_pro_country } root = { set_variable = sakuya_b5_swap_to_anti } }
				else_if = { limit = { is_political_lobby_type = lobby_anti_country } root = { set_variable = sakuya_b5_swap_to_pro } }
				else_if = { limit = { is_political_lobby_type = lobby_pro_overlord } root = { set_variable = sakuya_b5_swap_to_anti_overlord } }
				else_if = { limit = { is_political_lobby_type = lobby_anti_overlord } root = { set_variable = sakuya_b5_swap_to_pro_overlord } }
			}
		}
		if = {
			limit = { exists = scope:sakuya_b5_swap_lobby }
			scope:sakuya_b5_swap_lobby = {
				remove_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_lobby
				disband_political_lobby = yes
			}
			if = {
				limit = { has_variable = sakuya_b5_swap_to_anti }
				every_country = {
					limit = { any_political_lobby = { NOT = { has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_lobby } } }
					random_interest_group = { save_scope_as = sakuya_b5_swap_ig }
				}
				create_political_lobby = { type = lobby_anti_country target = scope:sakuya_b5_swap_target add_interest_group = scope:sakuya_b5_swap_ig lobby_formation_reason = funded }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { has_variable = sakuya_b5_swap_to_pro }
				random_interest_group = { save_scope_as = sakuya_b5_swap_ig }
				create_political_lobby = { type = lobby_pro_country target = scope:sakuya_b5_swap_target add_interest_group = scope:sakuya_b5_swap_ig lobby_formation_reason = funded }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { has_variable = sakuya_b5_swap_to_anti_overlord }
				random_interest_group = { save_scope_as = sakuya_b5_swap_ig }
				create_political_lobby = { type = lobby_anti_overlord target = scope:sakuya_b5_swap_target add_interest_group = scope:sakuya_b5_swap_ig lobby_formation_reason = funded }
			}
			else_if = {
				limit = { has_variable = sakuya_b5_swap_to_pro_overlord }
				random_interest_group = { save_scope_as = sakuya_b5_swap_ig }
				create_political_lobby = { type = lobby_pro_overlord target = scope:sakuya_b5_swap_target add_interest_group = scope:sakuya_b5_swap_ig lobby_formation_reason = funded }
			}
			remove_variable = sakuya_b5_swap_to_anti
			remove_variable = sakuya_b5_swap_to_pro
			remove_variable = sakuya_b5_swap_to_anti_overlord
			remove_variable = sakuya_b5_swap_to_pro_overlord
		}
	}
}

# === 按钮8: 强制请求结果 ===
sakuya_b5_lobby_force_accept = {
	scope = country
	is_shown = { is_player = yes }
	effect = {
		every_country = { every_political_lobby = { limit = { has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_lobby } change_appeasement = { amount = 5 factor = appeasement_lobby_request_accepted } } }
	}
}

sakuya_b5_lobby_force_ignore = {
	scope = country
	is_shown = { is_player = yes }
	effect = {
		every_country = { every_political_lobby = { limit = { has_variable = sakuya_b5_sel_lobby } change_appeasement = { amount = -5 factor = appeasement_lobby_request_ignored } } }
	}
}

# === 按钮9: 杠杆加速 ===
sakuya_b5_lobby_leverage_add = {
	scope = country
	is_shown = { is_player = yes }
	effect = {
		if = { limit = { NOT = { has_variable = sakuya_b5_lobby_leverage_mult } } set_variable = { name = sakuya_b5_lobby_leverage_mult value = 0 } }
		change_variable = { name = sakuya_b5_lobby_leverage_mult add = 1 }
		remove_modifier = sakuya_cheat_b5_lobby_leverage
		add_modifier = { name = sakuya_cheat_b5_lobby_leverage multiplier = var:sakuya_b5_lobby_leverage_mult }
		set_variable = sakuya_b5_lobby_leverage_active
	}
}

sakuya_b5_lobby_leverage_add_shift = {
	scope = country
	is_shown = { is_player = yes }
	effect = {
		if = { limit = { NOT = { has_variable = sakuya_b5_lobby_leverage_mult } } set_variable = { name = sakuya_b5_lobby_leverage_mult value = 0 } }
		change_variable = { name = sakuya_b5_lobby_leverage_mult add = 10 }
		remove_modifier = sakuya_cheat_b5_lobby_leverage
		add_modifier = { name = sakuya_cheat_b5_lobby_leverage multiplier = var:sakuya_b5_lobby_leverage_mult }
		set_variable = sakuya_b5_lobby_leverage_active
	}
}

sakuya_b5_lobby_leverage_sub = {
	scope = country
	is_shown = { is_player = yes }
	effect = {
		if = { limit = { NOT = { has_variable = sakuya_b5_lobby_leverage_mult } } set_variable = { name = sakuya_b5_lobby_leverage_mult value = 0 } }
		change_variable = { name = sakuya_b5_lobby_leverage_mult add = -1 }
		remove_modifier = sakuya_cheat_b5_lobby_leverage
		add_modifier = { name = sakuya_cheat_b5_lobby_leverage multiplier = var:sakuya_b5_lobby_leverage_mult }
		set_variable = sakuya_b5_lobby_leverage_active
	}
}

sakuya_b5_lobby_leverage_clear = {
	scope = country
	is_shown = { is_player = yes }
	effect = {
		remove_modifier = sakuya_cheat_b5_lobby_leverage
		remove_variable = sakuya_b5_lobby_leverage_mult
		remove_variable = sakuya_b5_lobby_leverage_active
	}
}
